 But then suddenly Mulayam did what was expected
 maujuudagi ne kayaas par viraam laga dieravivaar ko dilli ke jantar mantar main samaajawaadee party kii manch par mulaayam singh kii maujuudagi ne saare kayaas par viraam laga die
 As soon as Mulayam arrived, the happiness of Akhilesh's face was clearly visible and when the SP workers raised the slogan of 'prithvi' in the glory of Mulayam, 'prithviputra Mulayam Singh', Mulayam's soft smile was telling
 It was as if the father looked satisfied with his legacy
 hua bhi kuch aisa hi, mulaayam ne mike sambhala to sidhe kaha ki meri samaajawaadee party kabhi budhi naa ho ye meri ichha rahi he or aaj yahaan aap naujavaanon ko dekhakar lag rahaa he ki meri ichha puri ho rahi he
 What was there then, Akhilesh's face was not happy
 iske baad jaise hi akhilesh ne mike sambhala to sabase pehle kaha ki netaji ke aane se hamaare andar nai urja kaa sanchaar hua he
 Overall, Netaji not only stamped his legacy of SP in the hands of Akhilesh, but, according to his wishes, Akhilesh is also giving this message, pushing it forward

 patanjali kii sthapana yogaguru baba ramdev ke sahyog se varsh 2006 main kii gai, jo shampoo se lekar dantmanjan (toothpaste bhi) tak sab kuch banaati he
 
 
 Baba Ramdev may not have any stake in this kingdom of Ayurveda, which crossed the turnover of Rs 5,000 crore last year, but its face is the same
 
 
 patanjali ke chehre baba ramdev kii baalkrishna ke is kaarobaar main koi hissedari nahin Talking about shan-o-shaukat, a black-white rangerover car is seen around Balakrishna in the office, from which he moves from home to office, or from one part of Patanjali campus to another
 We do, because this campus in Haridwar is spread over 150 acres
 
 
 yah puche jane par ki kya unhen aaramdaayak sawari main anand aata he, unka jawaab tha, "car ke bare main nahin sochaa, suraksha ke bare main sochna behatar tha
 
 
 "on this Baba Ramdev said," i forced him to buy this car
 
 
 ham bahut yatra karte hai, or majboot car kii suraksha main rahanaa behatar hota he
 
 
 We do not care about expensive things
 
 
 " isi ke saath unhone behad saadhaaran-sa mobile phone bhi nikaalkar dikhaaya, jo unke mutabik 2,000 rupee kaa tha
 
 
 However Balkrishna admitted that he had an iphone
 
 
 donon mitron kii pehali mulaakaat aaj se 30 saal pehle haryana ke gurukul main hui thi, jahaan ve padhate the, or jald hi ve ek duusare ke kareeb aa gaye the
 
 
 Balkrishna is shy, Baba Ramdev is media-friendly
 
 
 baalkrishna kuch mote hai, jabaki baba ramdev saikadon-hazaron logon yaa tivi camere ke saamne apane patale-duble sharir kii madad se kathin se kathin asana bhi aasaani se kar liya karte hai
 
 
 Their working relationship is also absolutely unique
 
 
 baba ramdev apane sabase kareebi sahyogi ko 'bijnes partner nahin, aadhyatmik dost' kahkar pukaarte hai, jabaki baalkrishna kehete hai, "hamaare bich board meeting jaisaa kuch nahin hota
 
 
 Sometimes he brings me an idea, and he knows in advance what i want
 
 
 " By the way, ideas always get mixed up on the go
 
 
 ab jeens ko dizine karne or unhen banane ke bare main hi lijie
 
 
 According to Balakrishna, "it was you that a journalist was interviewing Ramdev ji, and he wore jeans
" 
 
 unhone us par kuch kaha, to patrkaar ne mazaaq main kaha ki aap log inhen kyon nahin banaate, to hamane bhi sochaa - kyon nahin
 
 
 ? " bas, tabhi se jane-maane or trendi kahalaane vaale brandon kii taraf se sanyukt upkram lagane ke liye peshkashon kii baadh-si ai hui he
 
 
 Actually, behind the success of Patanjali, the emphasis has been on indigenous or home-built
 
 
 vaise, jeens main kya swadeshi he, puche jane par baalkrishna ne hansate hue kaha, "unhen sthaneey sabziyon se rang lekar ranga ja saktaa he
 
 
 " patanjali ke pramukh baalkrishna ke bare main kaha jaataa he ki unhone ek bhi din chuttee nahin lee Babak Ramdev conferred the honorable title of 'acharya' on Balakrishna, and is part of the tradition of Patanjali
 
 
 iske alaava yah bhi mashhoor he ki baalkrishna kabhi ek din kii bhi chuttee nahin liya karte
 
 
 While we were interviewing him, he was still busy preparing a new herbal park and museum at the headquarters in Haridwar
 
 
 tippaniyan Showing his brand new lab, Balakrishna said, "I want the best scientific support available for our research and development
 
 
 " or usee samay baahar un trakon kii line lagi hui thi, jo makkhan ko haridwar le jaaenge, jahaan usamen se ghi nikaala jayega
 By the way, the best selling product of Patanjali is Ghee
 
 
 aalochakon kaa kahana he ki baalkrishna ke khilaaf farzi passport (kyonki unke mata-pita nepal se hai) or shaikshik yogyataon (digriyon) se jude maamle band karwaane main baba ramdev kaa saath tathaa unke dwaara bhartiya janata party (bijepi) kaa prachaar kiya janaa kaam aayaa, jabaki ek maamle main to jaanch sibiai ke hawaale thi
 
 
 The condemners also say that it cannot be a mere coincidence that with the formation of the BJP government at the Center, Patanjali started touching the sky of progress
 
 
 lekin baalkrishna kaa kahana he, "is baat se koi fark nahin padataa ki centre sarkaar hamaare paksh main he
 
 
 We need more state government, which has always been against us
 
 
 " uttarakhand main sattarudh congress sarkaar ke bare main baat karte hue baalkrishna ne bataaya, "har choti se choti chiz ke liye, har anaapatti praaanpatr ke liye ve hamen pareshaan karte hai
 
 
 " agar shaan-o-shaukat kii baat karen, to daftar main maujuud baalkrishna ke aasapaas sirf kaale-safed rang kii ek rangerovar car nazar aati he, jisase vah ghar se daftar aate-jate hai, yaa patanjali parisar ke ek hisse se duusare main jaaya karte hai, kyonki haridwar main bana yah parisar 150 acre main failaa hua he
 
 
 Asked if he enjoys a comfortable ride, his answer was, "don't think about the car, it's better to think about safety
" 
 
 " is par baba ramdev ne kaha, "maine unhen majaboor kiya tha ki yahi car khariden
 
 
 We travel a lot, and it is better to stay under the protection of a strong car
 
 
 ham mahangi chizon kii parvaah nahin karte
 
 
 "with this, he also showed a very simple mobile phone, which according to him was Rs 2,000
 
 
 haalanki baalkrishna ne sweekaar kiya ki unke paas yphone he
 
 
 The two friends first met 30 years ago in Gurukul, Haryana, where they studied, and soon became close to each other
 
 
 baalkrishna sharmile hai, baba ramdev media-friendli hai
 
 
 Balkrishna is somewhat obese, while Baba Ramdev can easily perform even the toughest asanas with the help of his thin body in front of hundreds of thousands of people or TV cameras
 
 
 unka kaamkaaji rishta bhi bilkul anoothaa he
 
 
 Baba Ramdev calls his closest colleague a 'spiritual partner, not a business partner', while Balakrishna says, "there is nothing like a board meeting between us
" 
 
 kabhi-kabhi vah mere paas koi idia lekar aate hai, or vah pehle se jaanate hai ki mujhe kya chahie
 
 
 " vaise idia to kabhi bhi yun hi chalate-phirte mil jaaya karte hai
 
 
 Now let's think about designing and making jeans
 
 
 baalkrishna ke anusaar, "hua you tha ki ek patrkaar ramdev ji kaa intervyuu le rahaa tha, or usne jeens pahani thi

 ?" Just then, there have been a spate of offers to set up joint ventures on behalf of well-known and trendy brands
 
 
 darasal, patanjali kii kamyaabi ke peeche swadeshi yaa swadesh-nirmit par jor dena rahaa he
